For instance, the evaluation may occur every `10s`, `30s`, `1m`, `10m`, etc.\n28: \n29: Rules in different evaluation groups can be evaluated simultaneously.\n30: \n31: Rules within the same evaluation group can be evaluated simultaneously or sequentially, depending on the rule type:\n32: \n33: - **Grafana-managed** rules within the same group are evaluated concurrently—they are evaluated at different times over the same evaluation interval but display the same evaluation timestamp.\n34: \n35: -
